Animated #

Adds subtle animations to the background cells, to introduce some dynamics to the brand. Please use animations with caution to avoid user distraction.
It is also recommended to only use the property for three layer background cells.

Animations will be disabled if the user has set their system preferences to minimize non-essential motion. See prefers-reduced-motion for more information.
